[](https://www.quic.cloud)
# ERROR 520
The QUIC.cloud server hel229-hyb-worker.quic.cloud was not able to connect to the site's origin server.
2026-02-20 11:35:07 UTC
### Web Browser
### QUIC.cloud Node
### Origin Server
### Why did this happen?
This site is using [QUIC.cloud](https://www.quic.cloud/) CDN. This error indicates that our QUIC.cloud nodes were unable to reach the website’s origin server.
### If you're a visitor
Please try again later.
### If you're the website owner
Please verify that your **Connection Type to Origin** and **Server IP** are set correctly in the QUIC.cloud CDN Configuration.
See these additional [troubleshooting steps](https://docs.quic.cloud/troubleshooting/httperror/#520-origin-server-unavailable).

## FAQs
What is LeadMine? 
LeadMine is a powerful lead generation software to find any B2B leads and their email addresses. We have 200+ million business contacts which are collected from all over the public web.
What does the LeadMine Chrome Plugin do? 
[_LeadMine Chrome Plugin_](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/leadmine-prospector/cjfcggkodegcngbhenjoppjagififcpk) is designed to get leads from any corporate websites, and Google search results. With a single click, you can collect your leads and we will automatically find corporate email addresses of the leads. Then you can download your leads in CSV file from the LeadMine dashboard.  
  
You can [install LeadMine chrome plugin](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/leadmine-prospector/cjfcggkodegcngbhenjoppjagififcpk) from chrome web store.
Is there a free plan? 
Absolutely. Sign up and you will get 10 credits per month for free. A credit card isn't required to signup.
Why haven’t I gotten the 'email confirmation' email after sign up? 
Sometimes there might be some short delay in our mail server sending out the verification email. Other times, it may be that your email server marks it as spam, so please make sure to check the spam folder! If you do not get the verification email in a reasonable amount of time, please [contact us](https://www.leadmine.net/contact/).
What payment methods do you accept? 
We currently accept payments online by credit cards and PayPal. For annual payments we also accept bank transfers.

## Features That Drive Results
  * ### Identify your target audience
Find your perfect prospects for your outbound campaigns using advanced filtering. Filter by location, industry, size, title and more.
![feature 1](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E)
  * ### Run and track multiple campaigns
Run multiple campaigns at once to better understand what works best for you, A/B test your approach to improve your results.
![feature 2](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E)
  * ### Image and GIF hyper-personalization
Import your own image or use one from our library. Personalize each image at scale with your prospect’s logo, LinkedIn profile picture, name, company and more.
![feature 3](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E)
  * ### Powerful multi-step campaigns
Set complex flows by placing different steps and time delays between them as you see fit. Combine steps to connect, view, follow, message, email and InMail your prospects.
![feature 4](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E)
  * ### Handle conversations with Smart Inbox
Manage and reply to all of your prospects all in one inbox. Separate messages per campaign, label prospects, add notes, and use our unread filter to find any replies that slipped through the cracks.
![feature 5](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E)
  * ### Get analytics with real-time data
Create customized reports to gain intelligence on your results. Set your timeframe and which metrics you want to analyze with the ability to export the results.
![feature 6](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E)

Put your sales pipeline on autopilot by leveraging the only tool that automates LinkedIn + email + customer image personalization at scale. Leadscope is a premium LinkedIn automation software that helps you get more meetings with your targeted prospects. It is a cloud-based LinkedIn Automation Tool that automates your LinkedIn prospecting, LinkedIn connection requests, LinkedIn leads, and LinkedIn sales outreach with hyper-personalization and targeted campaigns for lead generation.

## Einzigartig am Markt
Maximiere deinen Vertriebserfolg mit **smarten, geprüften Leads**. Unser Tool verbindet präzise Zielgruppenanalyse mit sofort einsetzbaren Kontaktdaten – für **mehr Abschlüsse in weniger Zeit.**
Leads, die wirklich passen
Finde genau die Leads, die du brauchst – mit smarten Filtern. Spare dir irrelevante Treffer und konzentriere dich auf echte Potenziale, die zu 100 % passen.
Leads ohne Limit
Zugriff auf Millionen Unternehmen – in Deutschland und weltweit. Immer aktuell, sofort verfügbar und bereit für deinen Vertrieb.
Verifizierte Kontakte
Alle Daten werden automatisch und manuell validiert – für höchste Qualität und DSGVO-Konformität. Du bekommst nur geprüfte Kontakte, auf die du dich verlassen kannst.
KI-gestützte Logik
Unsere KI priorisiert die besten Leads für dich – schnell, gezielt und effizient. So findest du die richtigen Kunden mit minimalem Aufwand.
### Leadscraper in 90 Sekunden
## Definiere die Zielgruppe
Sag uns einfach, wen du suchst – z. B. „Marketingagenturen in München“ oder „IT-Dienstleister in NRW“, wer dein gewünschter Ansprechpartner ist und ob du zusätzliche Einschränkungen hast.  
  
Unsere AI versteht **natürliche Sprache** und erstellt daraus automatisch eine **präzise Suchanfrage** – ohne Filter, ohne Dropdowns, ohne Umwege.
###### Einfach mit Freitext starten
Schreibe in deinen eigenen Worten, wen du suchst – ganz ohne Dropdowns und Formularlogik.
###### **KI erkennt Muster & Merkmale**
Unsere AI analysiert deine Beschreibung und identifiziert automatisch relevante Branchen, Firmengrößen und Orte.
###### Maximale Kontrolle, minimale Komplexität
Du kannst deine Zielgruppe jederzeit verfeinern – mit klaren Angaben zu Region, Größe oder Schwerpunkt.

## Warum LeadScraper?
Während **klassische Datenbanken** dir verstaubte Kontaktlisten liefern, scrapen wir deine Daten in Echtzeit – **individuell, frisch und exklusiv für dich.**
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6820e588ed19e45df8ee7b75/6828c45d760cfcbf66a77b3a_Group%201000003096.svg)
###### KI-Power
Du gibst nur deine Idee ein, wir übernehmen den Rest.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6820e588ed19e45df8ee7b75/6828c59a44e1908b2e36f1e3_Group%20\(1\).svg)
###### Live-Daten
Keine statischen Listen. Jeder Datensatz wird frisch gescraped.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6820e588ed19e45df8ee7b75/6828c59a56864c03ad5017db_Vector%20\(1\).svg)
###### DSGVO-ready 
Ohne versteckte Datenquellen. Rein aus öffentlichen Quellen.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6820e588ed19e45df8ee7b75/6828c59bf4c97e2c522c6cd9_Group%201000003094.svg)
###### 1-Klick-Export
Leads als CSV oder Excel, perfekt für jedes System deiner Wahl.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6820e588ed19e45df8ee7b75/6828c59da406b7094b898166_Group%201000003095.svg)
###### ROI-Rechner
Sofort sehen, wie viel Umsatz-Potenzial in deinen Leads steckt.

Nur relevante Unternehmen & Entscheider, die zu euch passen.

## Noch Fragen?
Hier findest du alles, was du vor dem Start mit LeadScraper wissen solltest.   
  
Solltest du weitere Fragen haben, dann freuen wir uns auf deine Nachricht unter **info@leadscraper.de**
**Ist es schwierig, den AI Scraper zu benutzen?**
Ganz im Gegenteil – **Leadscraper ist bewusst radikal einfach gehalten**.  
‍  
Statt komplizierter Filter oder endloser Dropdowns gibst du nur **drei einfache Datenfelder** ein: Zielgruppe, Region und gewünschte Leadanzahl. **Den Rest übernimmt die AI – automatisch und in Sekunden.  
‍**  
Keine Schulung nötig, keine technischen Hürden. Einfach starten, relevante B2B-Leads erhalten und direkt loslegen. 
**Woher stammen die Daten – und sind sie DSGVO-konform?**
Leadscraper nutzt eine Kombination aus öffentlich zugänglichen Webquellen, Unternehmensverzeichnissen, Branchenportalen und eigenen **AI-basierten Datenaufbereitungsverfahren**.   
  
Unser **AI-Scraper durchsucht in Echtzeit das Internet** nach B2B-relevanten Informationen und extrahiert ausschließlich **legal zugängliche Geschäftsdaten** – wie Firmennamen, Websites, Ansprechpartner oder Standorte. Alle Daten werden **DSGVO-konform** erhoben, verarbeitet und bereitgestellt.   
  
Wir legen höchsten Wert auf **Datenschutz** , Transparenz und Rechtssicherheit – damit du hochwertige B2B-Leads generieren kannst, ohne dir über rechtliche Fallstricke Gedanken machen zu müssen.
**Kann ich die Leads in mein CRM exportieren?**
Ja. Du kannst deine Leads ganz einfach als **CSV- oder Excel-Datei** exportieren – ideal für den Import in dein CRM oder Newsletter-Tool.  
  
‍**Direkt-Anbindungen** an alle gängigen Systeme sind in Planung, darunter: Dynamics, Hubspot, Pipedrive, Salesforce, Zoho CRM, Close & ActiveCampaign.  
  
Zusätzlich arbeiten wir an Integrationen mit **Zapier** , **Make (Integromat)** und **n8n** , um maximale Automatisierung und Flexibilität zu ermöglichen.
**Was ist der Unterschied zwischen einem Leadscraper und einer klassischen Leaddatenbank?**
Eine klassische Leaddatenbank bietet meist **vorgefertigte, statische Kontaktlisten** – oft veraltet, unpassend und nicht auf individuelle Zielgruppen zugeschnitten.  
  
Ein Leadscraper wie **Leadscraper.de** hingegen arbeitet dynamisch: Mithilfe künstlicher Intelligenz werden B2B-Daten **in Echtzeit** aus öffentlich zugänglichen Quellen extrahiert – präzise abgestimmt auf Ihre Zielgruppe, Branche und Region.  
  
‍**Das Ergebnis:** Keine generischen Listen, sondern **hochrelevante, aktuelle Leads** – automatisch selektiert und direkt einsatzbereit für deinen Vertrieb.
**Gibt es eine Mindestanzahl an Leads pro Bestellung?**
Nein. Du kannst **flexibel** **& günstig** starten – schon ab wenigen Leads. Perfekt zum Testen oder für gezielte Kampagnen. Du bestimmst das Tempo.
**Warum ein Leadscraper besser B2B Leads generieren kann als eine klassische Lead-Datenbank?**
Lead-Datenbanken liefern statische Kontakte – oft Monate oder Jahre alt. Ein Leadscraper generiert jede Anfrage **in Echtzeit** , auf Basis deiner Kriterien. Du bekommst keine alten Listen, sondern tagesaktuelle, individuell gefilterte Leads.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6820e588ed19e45df8ee7b75/68ba58bf48953947903f6d98_Group%201000003097%20\(1\).svg)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6820e588ed19e45df8ee7b75/68ba5b2b0139c232ae56a7db_Group%201000003097%20\(2\).svg)

## How much is missing data costing you?
Poor data hygiene costs your company up to 15% of your revenue. Every piece of data left uncaptured or entered poorly costs your team valuable insights and revenue. Automating data capture immediately after a meeting ensures your CRM is complete and accurate, preventing revenue from slipping through the cracks.

## Frequently Asked Questions
Get instant answers in our FAQ or connect with us via live chat! We're here to help.
Do you integrate with CRMs other than Salesforce & HubSpot?
[![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6741faaa0ab73dfc01ac6b27/674b521c1349b6e88aa5ff9b_%5BA%5D--faq-icon-wrap.svg)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6741faaa0ab73dfc01ac6b27/674b521c6aad6e56fb4aaeef_minus.svg)](https://www.leadbeam.ai/)
Yes. Leadbeam integrates with Salesforce, HubSpot, Pipedrive, Zoho CRM, and Microsoft Dynamics 365.  
Need something else? We can build custom CRM integrations within 24 hours.
Our CRM is customized. Can Leadbeam handle that?
[![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6741faaa0ab73dfc01ac6b27/674b521c1349b6e88aa5ff9b_%5BA%5D--faq-icon-wrap.svg)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6741faaa0ab73dfc01ac6b27/674b521c6aad6e56fb4aaeef_minus.svg)](https://www.leadbeam.ai/)
Yes, we can customize our app to fit your specific workflow.
Are you a CRM replacement?

PLATFORM
## We Automate Everything
From infrastructure to outreach — autonomous AI agents handle it all so you can focus on closing deals.
### Email Infrastructure
Dedicated IPs, real mailboxes, and enterprise-grade warmup. Your emails land in inbox, not spam.
### Lead Discovery
AI finds companies matching your ICP, extracts verified contacts, and refreshes data every quarter.
### AI Copywriting
Every email is unique. AI writes hyper-personalized messages based on company news, role, and pain points.
### Automated Outreach
Automated sequences with optimized timing, smart follow-ups, and response tracking. Runs 24/7/365.
#### Built-in CRM Included
Companies, contacts, deals, pipeline tracking, revenue forecasts — all in one place.

# Transform enablement from Passive to Active
**Letter AI gives revenue teams AI superpowers.** Deliver personalized content, learning, coaching, and buyer engagement that helps you win more, win better, win faster. Go from passive scavenger hunts to proactive value delivery with the world’s leading AI-native enablement platform.

It has made things possible that just weren't doable without AI, helping make the team more productive and win more customers.‍  
  
The quality of content is impressive and production ready, and the AI co-pilot is a game changer. Incredible platform!

# Frequently asked questions
Common questions asked about Letter AI
I’ve been sold the “unified enablement platform” story before. What’s different with Letter AI?
Letter AI distinguishes itself by combining the power of generative AI with your company’s specific documents and data to offer a truly unified revenue enablement platform. Unlike others, we deliver AI-powered content management and personalization alongside interactive training and coaching, in a single, deeply integrated platform where content informs training and vice versa.   
  
The Letter AI co-pilot brings it all together - providing a conversational entry point for your team to find everything they need. This integrated approach allows you to deliver revenue enablement in a single platform vs. multiple tools, resulting in cost savings and significantly enhancing the user experience.
How can Letter AI build enablement material in minutes?
Leveraging production-grade generative AI, Letter AI streamlines the creation of enablement materials by grabbing relevant knowledge and style from your existing documents and data and combining it with vetted external data. This AI-driven process ensures rapid delivery of rich multi-modal training and certification pathways. Combine that with rich learning insights and practical, hands-on activities evaluated in seconds with AI and you get impactful training built in minutes, not weeks or months.
How can I ensure the AI does not make things up (“hallucinate”)?
The Letter AI platform mitigates the risk of generating inaccurate or "hallucinated" content by anchoring its responses in your company's knowledge base, even declining to produce content when it cannot verify the necessary facts. This approach is underpinned by best-in-class AI engineering practices, a testament to the founding team's more than 20 years of experience in the field of artificial intelligence. On the very rare occasion that a hallucination slips through, the platform incorporates feedback loops that allow for the immediate reporting and correction of the issue, ensuring continual improvement and accuracy.
I have limited existing content. Can Letter AI still help me?
Absolutely, Letter AI is designed to work with varying levels of existing content. By utilizing AI-powered workflows, we can optimize and expand your resources, enabling the creation of interactive training, AI-powered coaching, collateral, and more. This approach has proven effective for our customers facing resource constraints, delivering significant improvements in content creation efficiency and effectiveness with minimal starting material.
How can I ensure the security of my data?
Letter AI prioritizes the security and privacy of our customers’ data through comprehensive security infrastructure and responsible data practices. Our security and privacy offerings are certified by the world’s leading security standards, such SOC 2 Type II. Furthermore, we never use AI models that train on your data, ensuring there is zero chance of leakage across different customer accounts. Beyond these measures, we offer enterprise-grade security measures such as customizable data retention policies, single sign-on (SSO), multi-factor authentication (MFA), and more.  
  
For more detailed information on how Letter AI protects user privacy and data, please visit our [Privacy & Security](https://www.letter.ai/data-and-security) page.

#### Privacy Overview
This website uses cookies to improve your experience while you navigate through the website. Out of these cookies, the cookies that are categorized as necessary are stored on your browser as they are essential for the working of basic functionalities...
Necessary 
Necessary
Always Enabled
Necessary cookies are absolutely essential for the website to function properly. This category only includes cookies that ensures basic functionalities and security features of the website. These cookies do not store any personal information. 
Non-necessary 
Non-necessary
Any cookies that may not be particularly necessary for the website to function and is used specifically to collect user personal data via analytics, ads, other embedded contents are termed as non-necessary cookies. It is mandatory to procure user consent prior to running these cookies on your website.

FAQ  

## Get all your questions answered here  

[Start for Free Now ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6894881c71dc9475b56935d5/6894881c71dc9475b56935ea_arrow-right.svg)](https://app.manyreach.com/e/signup)
What is a credit?
Get all your questions answered here Start for Free Now 1 credit means 1 email sent. If you have 1,000 credits, that means you can send 1,000 emails. Warmup emails also consumes credits on Pay As You Go plan 10 warmup emails = 1 credit. If you activate Power Mode you get unlimited warmups for free.
What do you mean by upload unlimited contact?
You can upload as many leads as you want in your Manyreach account. It doesn’t make sense for you to pay for just uploading all your leads in one place. Use Manyreach as your master database of all leads.
What all features do I get access to?
You get access to all the listed features without any monthly subscription. You can also get access to our power feature add-ons by paying a little extra a month.
When do my credits expire?
Credits resets every month. All unused credits are swapped with new set of credits depending on your lifetime plan.
Do you offer a free trial?
Yes, we offer a free plan. You get 250 credits to use on us.
How do you ensure my emails don’t go to spam?
Once you warmup your email accounts using Manyreach, we have a bunch of features like random delays, rotating IPs, mailbox rotation, spintax, timezone matching, auto-volume increasers, and more to make sure your emails are safe.
I have more questions. Where should I reach out?
Feel free to reach out via the chat icon on the bottom right of your screen. One of our support members would be happy to assist you shortly.

## Segurança em  
cada detalhe
Acesse nosso [Trust Center](https://trust.meetrox.ai/)
### Segurança e privacidade na prática
Seus dados ficam protegidos enquanto são enviados e também quando estão armazenados. Acesso é controlado por perfis e autenticação, com registros de atividade para auditoria. Cumprimos a LGPD e não usamos dados de clientes para treinar modelos externos.
### Governança e conformidade contínuas
Políticas definem por quanto tempo guardamos informações e quando elas são excluídas. Mantemos trilhas de auditoria, processo claro de resposta a incidentes e avaliação de fornecedores críticos. Segurança faz parte do dia a dia da operação.
### Transparência para decidir com confiança
Centralizamos políticas, perguntas frequentes, lista de suboperadores, status e documentos de segurança no nosso Trust Center. Seguimos referências do mercado como ISO 27001 e SOC 2 e publicamos atualizações de forma transparente.

### Membrain FAQ
Who is the Membrain B2B Growth Platform for?
Membrain is for B2B companies that are truly committed to growth, organizations that sell complex solutions, manage longer sales cycles, and navigate multiple stakeholders in every deal. It’s ideal for midsize to enterprise teams that rely on structure, methodology, and consistent execution to win high-value deals. If your sales success depends on guiding buyers through a multi-step decision process, Membrain is built for you. 
How will Membrain help me improve my sales effectiveness?
Membrain helps your team focus on the right activities and behaviors that actually move deals forward. It embeds your process, reinforces best practices, highlights risks early, and gives sales leaders clarity on where to coach. Instead of simply tracking what has happened, Membrain guides how to execute, improving consistency, forecast accuracy, deal quality, and overall sales performance. The result is stronger habits, better conversations, and more predictable growth across your entire organization. 
What makes Membrain different from other B2B Growth platforms?
Membrain is the only platform built around the idea that people are your most powerful growth engine. Our technology is designed to reinforce the right behaviors, guide your methodology, and make coaching and execution easier every day.  
What sets us apart:  

  * Technology built for complex B2B sales, not adapted from transactional CRMs
  * A global partner network of world-class sales trainers and experts who embed their methodologies directly into Membrain
  * A relentless focus on the human component, skills, behavior, alignment, and accountability
  * Deep support for execution, not just analytics
  * Founded in Sweden, with sales and customer success teams in Europe and the US to support your growth worldwide

  
The combination of technology, people, and process is what makes Membrain truly unique. 
Can I embed my sales methodologies or sales processes in Membrain?
Yes. Membrain is built precisely for that. You can embed your entire sales methodology, including stages, milestones, qualification criteria, content, workflows, and coaching prompts, directly into the platform. This turns your way of selling into a shared, guided framework that ensures consistency, clarity, and improved execution across every deal and every salesperson. 
What integrations does Membrain support?
Membrain integrates seamlessly with the essential tools your teams already use, including email and calendar systems, video and communication platforms, sales- and marketing tools. With an open API and Zapier support, Membrain can connect to hundreds of business applications to create a unified, efficient tech ecosystem that supports your entire sales process. 
How does Membrain handle data security and privacy?
Membrain is SOC2 Type 1 compliant, ensuring the highest standards of data security, availability, and confidentiality.

Person-level intent signals
Transforms social media interactions, reviews, and forum activity into actionable buying signals with real, contactable prospects.
Life event detection
Capture "Just moved to Austin" or "20 weeks pregnant" signals with verified contact info
Confidence scoring
Every signal includes timestamps and reason codes so you know exactly why someone was surfaced
People & Business Data Platform
Provides complete enrichment and identity resolution with unified people + business graph.
Complete identity graph
Social handles, verified contacts, work history, interests, and relationship networks
AI-ready architecture
Built specifically to provide context for agents and LLM workflows, not just CSV exports
How it works
We ingest public data, match it to our identity graph using AI, then deliver it through APIs for real-time.  
Docs: https://api.nyne.ai/documentation
01
Person data API's
Social profiles, verified contacts, work history, interests, and social connections
02

Ownership, decision makers, org structure, sentiment, and real-time engagement
03
Developer-first delivery

## Discover companies that are most similar to your best clients with AI
Oppwiser's AI Lookalike Company Finder feature helps businesses discover accounts that closely match their best clients. Focus your sales reps on accounts that are most likely to buy and improve sales pipeline velocity. 
[Learn more](https://oppwiser.com/ai-lookalike-company-finder)![](https://oppwiser.com/assets/img/main/arrow_forward_green.svg)
## Search for the top players in any niche or market with AI
Ditch limiting and clunky industry filters when researching companies. Use free text search to map out players in any industry, market, or niche. Additionally, apply advanced firmographic or keyword filters to pinpoint the companies that matter most. 
[Learn more](https://oppwiser.com/ai-lookalike-company-finder)![](https://oppwiser.com/assets/img/main/arrow_forward_green.svg)
## Map your Target Addressable Market in seconds
Opportunity Scanner will continuously scan a database of 60M+ companies and score each company based on its similarity to your existing clients or best prospects. Easily uncover net new accounts or identify high-intent lookalike accounts that may be buried in your CRM. 
[Learn more](https://oppwiser.com/ai-opportunity-scanner)![](https://oppwiser.com/assets/img/main/arrow_forward_green.svg)
## Spot buying and technographic signals within job offers, company, and employee data
Track any signal, technology, or keyword within job offers, public company data, and employee work experience. Uncover technology stacks, company, and work environment trends that you might be able to address with your offering or by tailoring your outreach. 
[Learn more](https://oppwiser.com/buyer-signals)![](https://oppwiser.com/assets/img/main/arrow_forward_green.svg)
## Get in touch with the right decision makers
Utilize a database of 150 million work emails and 10 million direct dials to connect with the buyers that matter most. Filter contacts by their work experience, education, location, and other data points. 
[Learn more](https://oppwiser.com/b2b-company-contact-data)![](https://oppwiser.com/assets/img/main/arrow_forward_green.svg)
![500x500](https://oppwiser.com/assets/img/index/verified_emails.png)
## Verified contact data
The deliverability of our email data is verified publicly as well as using SMTP check. All emails are marked as either valid or catch-all to identify if they are safe to send emails to.

#### One AI-powered platform for revenue teams.
Workflow first, results driven, and built to orchestrate every stage of the sales process.
1
Increase the number of reps hitting quota faster
Keep teams focused on selling with AI Agents that surface best-fit prospects, automate research, and recommend next best actions to increase productivity across every rep. 
2
Build and align stronger buying committees
Identify and engage all stakeholders with AI-powered account insights that align teams around buyer priorities, reduce friction, and improve win rates. 
3
Close more deals, faster
Rapidly inspect every deal in your pipeline with the AI Revenue Workflow Platform to uncover risks, prioritize actions, and accelerate deal velocity. 
4
Coach smarter and scale impact
Use AI-driven conversation insights to spot coaching opportunities in real time, deliver consistent feedback, and improve team-wide performance. 
5
Forecast with confidence
Reduce prep time and improve forecast accuracy with AI-assisted modeling that validates calls, compares outcomes, and drives revenue predictability. 
6
Retain and expand smarter with AI
Align sales, success, and account teams with AI-driven orchestration that flags renewal risks early, automates retention plays, and accelerates customer expansion.

###  Manage Consent Preferences
#### Strictly Necessary Cookies
Always Active
These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.
Cookie Details
#### Performance Cookies
Performance Cookies
These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.
Cookie Details
#### Functional Cookies
Functional Cookies
These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.
Cookie Details
#### Targeting Cookies
Targeting Cookies
These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## Effortless Outselling Experience
Outsell delivers a streamlined sales experience, providing free, high-quality contact data on LinkedIn and Salesforce. Discover leads at lightning speed, eliminate wasted time, and shift your focus to closing deals, all with the convenience of our easy-to-use Chrome Extension. 
![Image](https://outsell.ai/assets/img/illustrations/rocket_launch.svg)
  1. 1
#### Download Chrome Extension
Simply download Outsell's Chrome Extension and integrate it with your LinkedIn and Salesforce accounts for a smooth, unified experience. 
  2. 2
#### Uncover Opportunities
Leverage Outsell's high-quality, free contact data to swiftly identify and connect with potential leads, supercharging your sales pipeline. 
  3. 3
#### Close More Deals

Our business model is really simple. We want to provide a lot of features for free and, in the future, provide premium features to large enterprises. This model has been successfully proven for companies such as Dropbox.

## Capture & Nurture
How it starts: Transform static content into AI-driven interactive journeys that prospects want to engage with.
Stop losing prospects to generic forms and static PDFs. Create personalized interactive journeys that adapt to each visitor—capturing information progressively as they engage with content tailored to their role and buying stage.
Your ABM targets and demand gen traffic follow connected content paths that reveal buying intent and build momentum toward sales conversations—delivering 10x more qualified leads from the same marketing spend.

![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef357bef3ab9392cb6027e/f979406d-1a04-4f4c-8cf3-506cb5296fb0?tr=w-1258,h-766,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-1920,c-at_max)
![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef357bef3ab9392cb6027e/f979406d-1a04-4f4c-8cf3-506cb5296fb0?tr=w-1250,h-718,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-1920,c-at_max)
How sales takes over: Your team operates with AI-powered intelligence at every touchpoint.
Sales teams instantly find the right content through natural conversation—no more digging through folders. Ask “Show me what closes healthcare CFOs” and get exactly what you need, then create deal rooms where prospects engage with content and collaborate on buying decisions.
AI analyzes deal patterns, flagging at-risk opportunities while recommending exact content combinations that moved similar deals to closed-won. Engagement signals reveal which deals are advancing and which need intervention—turning buyers into advocates.
![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef357bef3ab9392cb60282/1582f265-6696-40e9-a24a-2ed73f090027?tr=w-338,h-68,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-384,c-at_max)
![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef357cef3ab9392cb60285/a3f7977f-c39c-4dd3-9432-c617796f29a9?tr=w-260,h-100,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-384,c-at_max)
![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef3576ef3ab9392cb60241/9781e1cf-83e0-4118-9d23-43dd988ba115?tr=w-174,h-174,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-256,c-at_max)
![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef3577ef3ab9392cb6024b/fffdf7ba-bc97-4b60-a6bb-a45eb1bd3798?tr=w-450,h-92,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-640,c-at_max)

![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef357cef3ab9392cb60287/50ec9dc5-f134-4b11-a056-213c67c2d83f?tr=w-160,h-232,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-256,c-at_max)
![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef357bef3ab9392cb6027e/f979406d-1a04-4f4c-8cf3-506cb5296fb0?tr=w-1240,h-720,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-1920,c-at_max)
![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef3576ef3ab9392cb60245/125949d5-1de3-4d6d-aaef-8bd938902b68?tr=w-110,h-118,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-128,c-at_max)
How reps win more: Agentic AI coaches transform every rep into a top performer.
Deploy intelligent coaching agents that analyze performance gaps, create personalized training paths, and deliver learning moments when needed. AI converts battle cards into digestible audio talks as podcasts or TED style talks while providing live deal support that matches conversation context to your knowledge base and delivers responses directly to reps’ screens.
Practice with hyper-realistic AI buyers simulating real scenarios—angry prospects, skeptical CFOs, renewal objections—then get scored feedback to master every conversation type. AI generates personalized simulations based on lost deals, creating adaptive learning loops that prevent repeated mistakes.
![](https://ik.imagekit.io/zvzrxdvzjue/6839aa9cb7b69e6f13c0ab50/images/68ef3577ef3ab9392cb6024b/fffdf7ba-bc97-4b60-a6bb-a45eb1bd3798?tr=w-450,h-92,c-force:q-80,f-webp:w-640,c-at_max)

# Keep Your CRM Pulse Strong with Mass Data Enrichment

**Redefine your CRM data hygiene today and watch your business thrive.**
Good data hygiene isn’t just about keeping things clean—it’s about maintaining real connections. Outdated data is like navigating with a blindfold, costing you valuable opportunities. PipeLaunch Signals ensures your CRM is always up-to-date, empowering you to stay ahead, seize new opportunities, and engage effectively with your customers and prospects. Let us be your guiding light in a data-driven world.

Timely information is everything. Whether it’s a new promotion, a company relocation, or an emerging risk, PipeLaunch Signals keeps you informed with real-time notifications on the events that drive your business. Respond faster, seize opportunities, and stay ahead of your competition—because with us, you’ll never miss a beat.

PipeLaunch provides the gold standard in data quality, ensuring your AI-driven strategies are built on a solid foundation for long-term success. Prepare for the future, today.

## Optimize your sales process  

Supercharge every step of your sales cycle and empower your team to win deals.  

Easily manage leads and dealsOne space for all your sales activitiesAutomate and scaleInstant sales insightsEnhance your CRM experience
![](https://www-cms.pipedriveassets.com/brand-half-page-illustrations/Leads-inbox-450.svg)
### **Easily manage leads and deals**
Organize customer data and interactions in one simple tool and act fast when opportunity strikes.
  * **Customize your pipelines**


Pipedrive’s kanban-style dashboard lets you visualize your sales funnel. Adjust your pipelines to your sales process and move deals along as they progress. We’ll notify you when you need to follow up.
  * **Centralize your sales data and contact history**  



Import data from spreadsheets or other pipeline management software in just a few clicks. Link products or services to deals to track negotiations and see the bigger picture.
  * **Add custom fields**


Shape your CRM to your business with custom fields. Capture must-have info for your sales team and automate calculations with smart formulas.  

[Learn more](https://www.pipedrive.com/en/products/sales/leads)
![](https://www-cms.pipedriveassets.com/cdn-cgi/image/quality=70,format=auto/https://www-cms.pipedriveassets.com/brand-half-page-illustrations/Sales-activities-450.png)
### One space for all your sales activities
Easily track sales conversations and tasks in one tool, giving your salespeople the context they need to follow up faster.
  * **Your one-stop sales inbox**


Speed up response time and never miss an opportunity again with two-way email sync. Connect up to five email accounts and keep prospects hooked with customizable templates.
  * **Calendar sync and task reminders**  



Manage your schedule from the comfort of your CRM. Calendar sync lets you link your business calendar to Pipedrive and reminds you of upcoming deadlines, helping you stay focused.
  * **Easy call scheduling**


Share your availability with leads and let them book calls on their schedule. Instantly generate meeting links for Google Meet, Zoom or Microsoft Teams.  

[Learn more](https://www.pipedrive.com/en/products/sales/email-and-communications)
![](https://www-cms.pipedriveassets.com/brand-half-page-illustrations/Automations-450.svg)
### **Automate and scale**
Streamline your sales process and use AI – get more done with less work.
  * **Automate your entire sales cycle**


Cut admin time in half and let reps focus on closing deals. Easily set up workflow automations for your team or choose from ready-made templates.
  * **Automate lead routing and increase conversion**  



[Automatically assign](https://pipedrive.com/en/blog/automatic-assignment) leads while they’re hot with custom rules. As they move through your sales funnel, Pipedrive will hand them off from one sales rep to the next so you can keep the ball rolling.
  * **Boost productivity with automated follow-ups**


Keep leads and prospects engaged with sales automation. Set up auto-sequences that trigger based on email interactions or use AI prompts to quickly respond to leads.  

[Learn more](https://www.pipedrive.com/en/products/sales/automations)
![](https://www-cms.pipedriveassets.com/brand-half-page-illustrations/Sales-assistant_2024-02-16-104401_vcwh.svg)

Take advantage of Pipedrive’s precise, real-time data analytics to track sales metrics and fine-tune your strategy.
  * **Monitor sales performance**


Set goals and measure progress with visual reports and dashboards. Quickly identify bottlenecks to keep your pipeline running smoothly.
  * **Forecast and track revenue**  



Confidently predict earnings based on past performance, from recurring revenue to one-off deals. Gain a comprehensive view of predicted income, allowing for quick, tactical adjustments.
  * **Get smarter, actionable insights**


Pipedrive’s AI Sales Assistant predicts which deals you’re most likely to win, or lose. Get suggestions on which leads to pursue, along with daily snapshots of your sales team’s performance.

## CRM FAQs
  * What is Pipedrive?
Pipedrive is a sales pipeline CRM designed to help small businesses manage leads, track sales activities and close more deals.
  * How does Pipedrive work?
In a nutshell, Pipedrive enables sales teams in small businesses to:
    * Streamline processes and consolidate sales data in one unified CRM sales tool.
    * Automate follow-ups and ensure timely responses to leads.
    * Keep an eye on sales achievements and assess team performance for ongoing improvement.
  * How to set up Pipedrive?
Setting up Pipedrive is straightforward. To get up and running with our CRM [pipeline management](https://www.pipedrive.com/en/features/pipeline-management) tool, here’s a brief guide:
    * Begin by importing existing data or building your leads database within Pipedrive’s sales CRM software. Explore our Marketplace integrations to infuse your pipeline with even more quality leads.
    * Define your sales pipeline, create active deals, synchronize your business email and calendar and start scheduling your next activities.
    * If collaboration is key, set up team access. Pipedrive offers granular permissions, allowing you to fine-tune who can view or modify your CRM data.
    * As you progress, keep a close eye on your sales outcomes by creating real-time reports and dashboards. This will help you adapt and refine your strategies for even greater success.
  * How will Pipedrive’s CRM solution help me improve sales?
Pipedrive’s CRM sales pipeline makes customer relationship management a breeze by allowing you to track leads, spot opportunities, measure key activities, streamline sales workflows and focus on sales success.
Automated reminders and follow-ups increase your productivity, eliminating repetitive, time-consuming tasks. Real-time reports show your sales reps and sales managers which business processes to prioritize.
  * Will Pipedrive work for a big team?
Yes! Pipedrive’s sales CRM software is well-suited for startups and larger teams alike.  
Our pipeline CRM helps large sales and marketing teams streamline their customer interactions. Sales managers and their teams can benefit from a progress tracker, sales automation, procession forecasting, an activity-based planner and top security.
In addition, large teams have access to a dedicated account manager to help them make the most of Pipedrive. Your account manager can also help you onboard other team members to your sales CRM system and guide you on [pipeline management](https://www.pipedrive.com/en/features/pipeline-management) best practices.


  * What does CRM stand for in sales?
“CRM“ in sales stands for “Customer relationship management.” Although the “C” in “CRM” stands for “customer,” the best CRM tools can help teams enhance every stage in the sales cycle.
  * What is a CRM in sales?
A CRM, or sales CRM tool, is a system sales teams use to manage customer data and nurture customer relationships. Several popular CRM and sales tools exist on the market, including Pipedrive.
  * How does CRM help sales?
A CRM for sales enables you and your reps to centralize contact information, track ongoing activities and boost customer retention. Pipedrive’s visual sales pipeline lets you see your entire sales cycle at a glance, highlighting key opportunities. Get notified when you need to follow up, helping you enhance your customer experience and drive more deals than ever.
  * What is CRM software?
CRM software is the technology organizations use to manage relationships and business processes. Typically, CRM software for sales teams lets users track their activities, manage communications with other parties, measure individual and team progress and forecast revenue. The top CRM sales software integrates with other business tools, such as email marketing, document management and website tracking software.
  * How do I choose a CRM?
Choosing a good CRM sales tool for your business requires research and testing. Many companies, including Pipedrive, offer new users a 14-day free CRM trial to see if the software suits their needs. When searching for the best CRM software, consider ease of use, onboarding and results orientation. You should also look for the best pipeline management software and [sales management software](https://www.pipedrive.com/en/features/sales-management-software) to ensure your CRM has all the functionality your team needs to drive business growth.
  * Which apps can I connect with Pipedrive?
Pipedrive integrates with hundreds of tools and apps through the Pipedrive Marketplace, including Facebook, Zapier, Xero, Trello and Zoom. You can find Pipedrive integrations with lead generation software, sales and marketing tools, video calling apps, customer support solutions and social media platforms.

## Privacy Preference Center
When you visit any website, it may store or retrieve information on your browser, mostly in the form of cookies. This information might be about you, your preferences or your device and is mostly used to make the site work as you expect it to. The information does not usually directly identify you, but it can give you a more personalized web experience. Because we respect your right to privacy, you can choose not to allow some types of cookies. Click on the different category headings to find out more and change our default settings. However, blocking some types of cookies may impact your experience of the site and the services we are able to offer.   
[More information](https://www.pipedrive.com/en/privacy)
Allow All
###  Manage Consent Preferences
#### Performance Cookies
Always Active
These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.
#### Targeting Cookies
Always Active
These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.
#### Functional Cookies
Always Active
These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.
#### Strictly Necessary Cookies
Always Active
These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

Frequently asked questions
### Everything else you need to know
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6560f3502c15faf9c381ec8e/683c47348875d9729edd0250_lines.svg)
What is PlusVibe?
PlusVibe is an AI-driven cold email automation and deliverability platform designed to help businesses send outreach at scale while maximizing inbox placement.
How do I get started with PlusVibe?
Sign up with our free [14-day trial](https://app.plusvibe.ai/v2/register/) or [schedule a demo call](https://calendly.com/piplcampaign/talk-to-ceo) with our sales team.
Is PlusVibe suitable for businesses of all sizes?
Yes — PlusVibe works for solo founders, small teams, agencies, and large sales orgs.  
‍  
Whether you're sending 50 emails a week or managing 500 inboxes, the platform scales with you — no complex setup or technical overhead required.
How does the email warming feature work?
PlusVibe’s warming system sends and replies to emails across a private network of verified inboxes — building trust with inbox providers like Gmail and Outlook.  
  
It simulates natural human behavior (sends, opens, replies, stars) to boost your sender reputation and avoid spam folders — automatically, with no setup needed.  
  
All warmup activity runs through isolated, secure infrastructure, not shared public pools. That means your domain and inboxes are never exposed to third-party tools or toxic IP networks.
How does PlusVibe prevent emails from landing in spam?
PlusVibe is built from the ground up for deliverability. Here’s how we keep you out of spam:  
  
- **Auto-configured domains** with proper SPF, DKIM, and DMARC  
- **Private warm-up pool** that builds sender reputation safely  
- **Smart sending logic** — throttled volume, inbox rotation, reply detection  
- **No open tracking by default** — protects your domain reputation  
- **Deliverability monitor** to alert you before issues happen  
  
Everything’s optimized behind the scenes so your emails land where they should — in inboxes, not junk folders.
How do I scale my outreach with PlusVibe?
Scaling with PlusVibe is simple and safe:  
  
- Spin up dozens (or hundreds) of ready-to-send inboxes — no tech setup needed  
- Use our Chrome extension to scrape leads  
- Personalize messages at scale with AI-powered first lines and variables  
- Run smart, multi-inbox campaigns with reply tracking and auto-labeling  
- Let the AI Reply Agent handle responses, so you focus on qualified leads
Is PlusVibe GDPR and CAN-SPAM compliant?
Yes — PlusVibe is designed to support compliant outreach:  
  
- You control and manage your contact data at all times  
- Every email includes automatic unsubscribe and sender details  
- We don’t store or sell personal lead data — all enrichment is user-triggered  
- Warm-up and sending infrastructure is secure, private, and fully opt-in  
  
It’s your responsibility to follow laws in your region, but PlusVibe gives you all the tools to stay compliant while scaling responsibly.
Is there customer support available?
Yes — PlusVibe offers multiple ways to get help:  
  
- **Live chat support** right inside the platform  
- [**1:1 onboarding calls**](https://calendly.com/piplcampaign/talk-to-ceo) to get your setup dialed in  
- Access to our [**Cold Outreach Academy**](https://help.plusvibe.ai/en/) and strategy resources  
- Join the [**Slack community**](https://join.slack.com/t/pipl-ai/shared_invite/zt-34ur4zxps-5xe5yqABUDSvzt3NSSFycw) to learn from other users and share wins  
  
You're never on your own — we’re here to help you scale.
